# Aerulean Concordium / Gilded Covenant event chain

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# 100001 - The Rainbow Petition Found
# ---------------------------------------------------------
character_event = {
    id = aerulean_mod.100001
    hide_window = no

    trigger = {
        # Trigger on ruler of Aerulean faith, prestige threshold to make it visible
        is_ruler = yes
        has_faith = aerulean_overhaul
        prestige = 500
    }

    title = "aerulean_mod.100001.t"
    desc = "aerulean_mod.100001.d"

    option = {
        name = "aerulean_mod.100001.a_purge"
        # Execute or otherwise remove leadership: makes Concordium violent -> strong justification
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
        add_prestige = 100
        # flag to mark the leadership knocked out (used later to reform)
        set_global_flag = concordium_leadership_smashed
        # escalate unrest -> spawn loyalists/underground cells
        every_character = {
            limit = { has_faith = aerulean_overhaul }
            random = { chance = 10 add_character_modifier = concordium_supporter } # seeds sympathizers
        }
        news_event = { id = aerulean_mod.100001.1 scope = ROOT }
    }

    option = {
        name = "aerulean_mod.100001.b_imprison_reform"
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
        add_prestige = 25
        # imprison leaders and later reform Concordium into your propaganda arm
        set_global_flag = concordium_leadership_imprisoned
        # temporarily reduce unrest; mark reformation pending
        add_council_power = -10
        news_event = { id = aerulean_mod.100001.2 scope = ROOT }
    }

    option = {
        name = "aerulean_mod.100001.c_ignore"
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
        add_piety = -10
        # ignoring lets them radicalize faster
        set_global_flag = concordium_ignored
        news_event = { id = aerulean_mod.100001.3 scope = ROOT }
    }
}

5) Propaganda / Newspaper mechanics explained (how to simulate a newspaper)
CK3 doesnâ€™t have a direct â€œnewspaperâ€ object, so simulate it like this:

Use a recurring event (100050) that quietly seeds the concordium_propaganda modifier on random courtiers, bishops, and mayors.

Those courtiers then act as nodes of sympathy: they can spread the concordium_supporter modifier (via other events), be used as triggers for local unrest, or be targeted in your purge decisions.

When you choose â€œreform/co-optâ€ in the Rainbow Petition flow, you set concordium_reformed_by_crown â€” this enables the recurring propaganda event (100050) to fire and seed more modifiers. You can tune frequency by re-invoking the event from a decision or from a on_yearly_pulse hook for performance control.

If you prefer a more deterministic spread, replace random = { chance = X } with a list that targets specific counties, courtiers, or a percentage of realm vassals.

7) Implementation notes & tuning tips
To make the Concordium grow more violent and unstable over time: chain events which check has_character_modifier = concordium_supporter plus years_passed or global_flag checks, and each time they escalate they get a stronger modifier (replace concordium_supporter with concordium_extremist giving them -opinion with ruler and positive zeal for reforms). This gives you a neat justification for escalating punishments.

If you want newspapers to have geographic spread, add target filters in the recurring event like is_in_realm = ROOT or region = <your region tag>.

If your â€œElf Destinyâ€ system already grants immortal life, ensure your transcended_elf trait is the flag your other code looks for. If not, I can write a small hook that grants immortality via a custom flag or via an on_action that prevents death.

1) Purge / Execute vs Smash â€” what they mean (lore & mechanical)
Purge / Execute (targeted)

Mechanical effect: sets a flag (e.g. concordium_leadership_smashed / concordium_leaders_removed), removes leadership-level modifiers/traits, seeds paranoia and underground cells. Leaves the idea and grassroots sympathizers alive and able to reconstitute.

Smash (total destruction)

TL;DR: Purge/execute is targeted and creates useful justification & future gameplay (underground cells, propaganda opportunities). Smash is absolute removal; simpler but less long-term emergent drama.

1) common/modifiers/numenor_modifiers.txt
Path: common/modifiers/numenor_modifiers.txt
Paste this entire block into that file.

########################################
# Num enor â€” Concordium & Bias Modifiers
# file: common/modifiers/numenor_modifiers.txt
########################################

numenor_concordium_supporter = {
    opinion = {
        who = culture_group:elven_group
        value = 10
    }
    monthly_prestige = 0.5
}

numenor_concordium_propaganda = {
    # Represents a newspaper / pamphlet aura that increases local sympathy
    opinion = {
        who = culture_group:elven_group
        value = 5
    }
    monthly_prestige = 0.25
}

numenor_concordium_reformed = {
    # Holder is a managed/propaganda cell loyal to the ruler's version of the Concordium
    opinion = {
        who = ROOT
        value = 25
    }
    monthly_prestige = 1.0
}

# Cultural / religious bias modifiers (used when seeding/opinion checks)
numenor_respects_oldfaiths = {
    opinion = {
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                religion_group = pagan_group
                religion_group = jewish_group
                religion_group = zoroastrian_group
            }
        }
        value = 15
    }
}

numenor_distrusts_foreign_mortals = {
    opinion = {
        trigger = {
            OR = {
                culture_group = arabic_group
                culture_group = turkic_group
                culture_group = mongolic_group
                culture_group = indian_group
                culture_group = berber_group
                culture_group = west_african_group
                culture_group = east_african_group
                culture_group = chinese_group
            }
        }
        value = -40
    }
}

numenor_non_aerulean_envy_elves = {
    opinion = {
        trigger = { culture_group = elven_group }
        value = -30
    }
}
2) common/on_actions/numenor_on_actions.txt
Path: common/on_actions/numenor_on_actions.txt
This seeds supporters on character creation and hooks into yearly pulse for propaganda. Paste the block below.

########################################
# Num enor â€” On actions hooks
# file: common/on_actions/numenor_on_actions.txt
########################################

on_character_created = {
    # small chance new characters in Numenor get seeded with concordium sympathy
    if = {
        has_faith = aerulean_overhaul
        random = { chance = 5 }
        add_character_modifier = numenor_concordium_supporter
    }
    # give cultural bias to non-elves regarding envy of elves
    if = {
        NOT = { has_faith = aerulean_overhaul }
        add_character_modifier = numenor_non_aerulean_envy_elves
    }
}

on_yearly_pulse = {
    # if propaganda organ active, run the yearly news seeding
    if = { global_flag = numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown }
    events = { numenor_mod.500200 } # yearly propaganda seed
}

4) common/decisions/numenor_decisions.txt
Path: common/decisions/numenor_decisions.txt
Contains decisions to reform the Concordium into a state organ and to smash it.

########################################
# Num enor â€” Decisions
# file: common/decisions/numenor_decisions.txt
########################################

decision = {
    id = NUMENOR_REFORM_CONCORDIUM
    potential = {
        is_ruler = yes
        has_faith = aerulean_overhaul
        global_flag = numenor_concordium_leadership_imprisoned
        NOT = { global_flag = numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown }
    }
    allow = {
        prestige = 100
    }
    effect = {
        set_global_flag = numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown
        every_character = {
            limit = { has_faith = aerulean_overhaul random = { chance = 8 } }
            add_character_modifier = numenor_concordium_reformed
        }
        add_piety = 30
        create_message = {
            title = "numenor_mod.decision.reform.t"
            desc = "numenor_mod.decision.reform.d"
        }
    }
    ai_will_do = { factor = 0.1 }
}

decision = {
    id = NUMENOR_SMASH_CONCORDIUM
    potential = {
        is_ruler = yes
        has_faith = aerulean_overhaul
        NOT = { global_flag = numenor_concordium_destroyed }
    }
    allow = {
        gold = 200
        prestige = 200
    }
    effect = {
        set_global_flag = numenor_concordium_destroyed
        every_character = {
            limit = { has_character_modifier = numenor_concordium_supporter }
            remove_character_modifier = numenor_concordium_supporter
        }
        every_character = {
            limit = { has_character_modifier = numenor_concordium_propaganda }
            remove_character_modifier = numenor_concordium_propaganda
        }
        add_prestige = 150
        create_message = { title = "numenor_mod.decision.smash.t" desc = "numenor_mod.decision.smash.d" }
    }
    ai_will_do = { factor = 0.0 }
}

6) events/numenor_quill_news_events.txt
Path: events/numenor_quill_news_events.txt
This is the Imperial Quill modular news framework; it will both seed propaganda (yearly) and provide several sample news articles that are triggered from common on_actions. Paste the block below into that file.

########################################
# Num enor â€” Imperial Quill news & propaganda
# file: events/numenor_quill_news_events.txt
# namespace: numenor_mod
########################################

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# 500200 - Yearly Propaganda Seed (auto-run by on_yearly_pulse)
# ---------------------------------------------------------
character_event = {
    id = numenor_mod.500200
    hide_window = yes

    trigger = {
        is_ruler = yes
        global_flag = numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown
    }

    immediate = {
        every_character = {
            limit = {
                has_faith = aerulean_overhaul
                is_in_realm = ROOT
                random = { chance = 6 }
            }
            add_character_modifier = numenor_concordium_propaganda
        }
        add_prestige = 10
    }

    option = { name = root ai_chance = { factor = 100 } }
}

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# 500300 - Imperial Quill: War Report (example)
# Call this from on_war_started or on_war_ended as needed:
# events = { numenor_mod.500300 }
# ---------------------------------------------------------
character_event = {
    id = numenor_mod.500300
    hide_window = no

    trigger = {
        is_ruler = yes
        global_flag = numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown
    }

    title = "numenor_mod.500300.t"
    desc = "numenor_mod.500300.d"

    option = { name = "numenor_mod.500300.a_close" ai_chance = { factor = 100 } }
}

# ---------------------------------------------------------
# 500310 - Imperial Quill: Festival / Speech (example)
# Call from relevant hooks (on_ruler_speech / on_festival_held)

8) Quick integration guide & usage notes
Paste / create files as above. Restart the game to load the mod. Use a unique .mod descriptor (or integrate into your master-patch descriptor).

Event triggering

The numenor_mod.500300 (war) and other Quill article events are modular examples. To auto-fire them on actual game actions you need to tie them to existing on_actions events:

Example (in common/on_actions/numenor_on_actions.txt) add:

on_war_started = { events = { numenor_mod.500300 } }
on_war_ended = { events = { numenor_mod.500300 } }
on_festival_held = { events = { numenor_mod.500310 } }
on_birthday = { events = { numenor_mod.500320 } }
on_character_crowned = { events = { numenor_mod.500300 } } # or another event
I added the yearly pulse hook already; if you want immediate news on those hooks, copy the above lines into your numenor_on_actions.txt. (Be careful: not all on_action hooks exist for every specific action; if a hook name is incorrect you can call the event manually from a scripted decision or another event.)

Concordium flow

When discovery event numenor_mod.500001 fires, choose how to act. If you later pick the decision NUMENOR_REFORM_CONCORDIUM (available after the imprisonment flag), it will set the numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown flag and begin seeding propaganda yearly and allow Quill events to appear.

NUMENOR_SMASH_CONCORDIUM removes modifiers and sets numenor_concordium_destroyed.

Transcended Trait

If you already have a system that grants immortality or other mechanics, tie checks to the transcended_elf trait. The example event earlier that added transcended_elf should be left only for narrative moments where you intend to create such beings (we've not included automated mass transformation here â€” humans still believe ascension is impossible).

Non-conflict notes

All flags, event ids, modifier names use numenor_ / numenor_mod prefixes and ids in the 500k range to minimize collisions. If your master patch also uses numenor_ you can rename the prefix quickly (find & replace).

If you already have aerulean_overhaul faith keys in master patch, these events assume that exact faith key (has_faith = aerulean_overhaul). If your master patch uses a different faith key, replace all instances of aerulean_overhaul with your actual faith ID.

Numenor Imperial Quill Module V1

Numenor â€” Imperial Quill Module (Dormant)
Purpose: Self-contained, dormant module that awakens when an empire title e_numenor is created. Provides:

The Imperial Quill news framework (modular news events triggered by public actions)

Concordium discovery / reform / propaganda flow

Decisions to reform or smash the Concordium

Propaganda seeding and yearly pulse for public news distribution

transcended_elf trait stub (connect to your Elf Destiny mechanics)

Midnight Court member trait buffs (highly buffed stat templates)

Safe framework for cultural/religious preference placeholders (no real-world traits included)

Architect-of-Wonders hooks and example news triggers

Module is dormant until the empire title e_numenor exists. This avoids naming your realm prematurely â€” activate when you form the empire.

How to install
Create a module folder (example):

<mod root>/numenor_imperial_quill/
  common/
    modifiers/
    on_actions/
    decisions/
    traits/
    scripted_triggers/
    scripted_effects/
  events/
  localization/english/
  README.txt
  descriptor.mod
Paste each file's content below into the indicated path. Restart the game after installing.

IMPORTANT: If your master patch already uses numenor_mod prefixes or e_numenor, rename the numenor_ prefixes consistently.

Files & Contents
All code blocks below are ready-to-paste into the exact file paths shown.

1) common/scripted_triggers/numenor_activation_triggers.txt
##########################################################
# numenor_activation_triggers.txt
# Trigger to detect if the empire we want exists
##########################################################

trigger = {
    is_numenor_founded = {
        has_title = e_numenor
    }
}

# Additional useful trigger examples
trigger = {
    is_numenor_ruler = {
        is_ruler = yes
        any_title = { has_title = e_numenor }
    }
}
These triggers are small helper templates you can reference in events/decisions (trigger = { is_numenor_founded = yes }).

2) common/modifiers/numenor_modifiers.txt
##########################################################
# numenor_modifiers.txt
##########################################################

numenor_concordium_supporter = {
    opinion = {
        who = culture_group:elven_group
        value = 10
    }
    monthly_prestige = 0.5
}

numenor_concordium_propaganda = {
    opinion = {
        who = culture_group:elven_group
        value = 5
    }
    monthly_prestige = 0.25
}

numenor_concordium_reformed = {
    opinion = {
        who = ROOT
        value = 25
    }
    monthly_prestige = 1.0
}

# Cultural preference placeholders (EMPTY by design)
# Fill these with your custom "aesthetic" groups later.
# DO NOT use real-world protected attributes. Use lore-friendly culture_group tags.
numenor_preference_1 = {
    opinion = { value = 0 }
}

numenor_dislike_1 = {
Note: diplomacy, stewardship, etc. in modifiers may not be used by all versions or may require interplay with other mods that read those fields. These act as flavor and will show as modifiers if supported by your mod stack. Adjust as needed.

3) common/traits/numenor_traits.txt
##########################################################
# numenor_traits.txt
# trait stubs for module
##########################################################

transcended_elf = {
    icon = theurgy
    is_good = yes
    stewardship = 2
    learning = 2
    prestige = 50
    desc = "transcended_elf_desc"
}

# Midnight Court exemplar trait â€” assign to named NPCs to make them 'perfect'
midnight_court_exemplar = {
    icon = intrigue
    is_good = yes
    monthly_prestige = 5.0
    stewardship = 4
    diplomacy = 6
    learning = 6
    martial = 4
    intrigue = 6
    prestige = 200
    description = "midnight_court_exemplar_desc"
}
Assign midnight_court_exemplar to your Midnight Covenant/Night Court members. They will be noticeably outstanding. Use sparingly to avoid game imbalance.

4) common/on_actions/numenor_on_actions.txt
##########################################################
# numenor_on_actions.txt
# seeds supporters and wires yearly pulse (dormant until e_numenor exists)
##########################################################

on_character_created = {
    if = {
        has_faith = aerulean_overhaul
        random = { chance = 5 }
        add_character_modifier = numenor_concordium_supporter
    }
    if = {
        NOT = { has_faith = aerulean_overhaul }
        add_character_modifier = numenor_non_aerulean_envy_elves
    }
}

on_yearly_pulse = {
    if = { is_numenor_founded = yes and = { global_flag = numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown } }
    events = { numenor_mod.500200 }
}

# Public hooks (Modular: only active once everking is crowned)
# These forward public major actions to the Imperial Quill news system
on_war_started = {
    if = { is_numenor_founded = yes and = { global_flag = numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown } }
    events = { numenor_mod.500300 }
}

on_war_ended = {
    if = { is_numenor_founded = yes and = { global_flag = numenor_concordium_reformed_by_crown } }
    events = { numenor_mod.500300 }
}

Integration notes & how it will feel in-game
Initiation flow: Use the NUMENOR_INITIATE_MIDNIGHT decision to select a courtier/maid (the game decision UI will let you pick a character). That decision triggers the initiation event which grants midnight_covenant_member + pale_lord. Theyâ€™ll be extremely powerful and loyal to you. Use sparingly (you said you wanted them perfect â€” now they are).

Missions: Use NUMENOR_MIDNIGHT_MISSION to choose mission type and target. Each mission triggers one of the events in the events file and resolves with either success or failure text and mechanical effects (opinion, prestige, hidden shadowed modifier). Mission outcomes are probabilistic for drama and emergent gameplay.

Control vs Emergence:

You control the initiation and direct missions.

The emergent vampiric nemesis cycle (Sanguine Blight / Pale Lords across the world) still runs via the global pulse we discussed earlier (the 50-year checks). That system will spawn rare Veil events elsewhere; the Midnight Covenant can be used to monitor, manipulate, or eliminate them â€” your tool for both order and subterfuge.

Piety & Faith: pale_lord and midnight_covenant_member are hidden traits; by default they can carry a slight piety penalty if you want (we did not force that here). If you want piety penalties (and rituals to recover piety), I can add those easily, or make the penalty conditional (e.g., only when your Areulean faith has certain tenets). You said you will be reforming Aerulean later â€” we can tie piety gain/penalty flips to those tenet decisions.

Small balance & safety notes
The midnight_covenant_member trait is intentionally very powerful. Use it carefully â€” assign only a handful of characters to keep the game balanced. If you want them even stronger, tell me and Iâ€™ll push stats further (with caution).

The â€œQuiet Removalâ€ event does not forcibly delete characters in the code above; it applies strong narrative consequences and prestige. If you prefer a harder mechanic (removal/imprisonment), we can add a conditional kill_character or imprison chain, but I kept it less destructive to avoid accidental save-breaking.

Everything here is fictional and in-game â€” nothing creates or describes real-world wrongdoing outside a fantasy RPG context.

Great â€” this is the exact kind of practical question you need answered before you paste more files into a huge mod list. Iâ€™ll give you a compact, tactical playbook you can follow right now to make sure the Midnight Covenant bits (and the rest of the Numenor Quill/AnÃ¡rion modules) actually sit nicely with the ~200 mods in your load order.

Iâ€™ll cover:

How CK3 loads and where conflicts come from

Concrete rules to avoid clashes (namespacing, IDs, localization)

How to structure the master patch so modules donâ€™t stomp on each other

A step-by-step testing & merge plan you can run locally

Quick fixes for common problems and tools/commands youâ€™ll use

Short version: use unique namespaces, donâ€™t overwrite vanilla/other mod files unless intentional, test small, iterate, and keep backups.

1) How CK3 loads files (why conflicts happen)
CK3 loads mods in the order listed in the launcher. For files with the same path/name, the last-loaded mod overrides earlier ones.

Most conflicts are caused by two mods defining the same key (event ID, trait name, localization key, or modifying the same vanilla file).

Localization is fragile: the same key defined twice will be overwritten by the last loaded mod.

Event ID collisions (e.g. mymod.1000) arenâ€™t enforced by CK3 â€” if two mods use the same ID, they conflict in unpredictable ways.

2) Concrete rules to avoid clashes (apply to every file you paste)
Namespacing & IDs
Prefix everything you add with a unique prefix: numenor_, numenor_mod., or anarion_.

Events â†’ numenor_mod.600xxx

Traits â†’ numenor_pale_lord (not just pale_lord)

Modifiers â†’ numenor_midnight_loyal

Decisions â†’ NUMENOR_INITIATE_MIDNIGHT

Use event ranges far from common mod ranges. Many mods use 1000-1500, so using 600000+ like we did is good. Keep events in a distinct block.

For localization, use a unique prefix: numenor_mod.twilight_ascendance.t rather than twilight_ascendance.t.

Files and paths
Donâ€™t edit vanilla files. Instead, create new files under the same folders in your mod (e.g., events/numenor_midnight_events.txt). That will append rather than replace.

If you need to patch a vanilla file, create a compatibility patch that explicitly replaces only the part you want â€” keep it minimal.

Localization
Prefix all keys. Use one file per language and keep your keys alphabetized so diffs are manageable.

Avoid reusing simple keys like yes, no, title_1. Always use numenor_mod.*.

Traits / Definitions
Keep trait, modifier, and variable names unique and remember to check your common folder for overlaps.

Mark private, secret traits as hidden = yes.

3) Structuring the master patch for modularity
Use a folder structure like:

master_patch/
  common/
    traits/numenor_vampiric_traits.txt
    modifiers/numenor_midnight_modifiers.txt
    variables/numenor_item_pools.txt
  events/numenor_midnight_events.txt
  decisions/numenor_midnight_decisions.txt
  localization/english/numenor_midnight_l_english.yml
  README.md
Keep each feature as its own file and name them by feature. That makes future merges simple.

Add a README.md documenting:

What the file contains

Any dependencies (e.g., Elf Destiny required for enchantress trait)

Flags you set (e.g., numenor_midnight_initialized)

Recommended load order positioning (e.g., â€œplace after Elf Destiny submodsâ€)

4) Step-by-step integration & testing plan (do this every time you add/modify)
Preparation
Backup your save & mod folder â€” copy your master_patch and current save before changes.

Create a test profile in CK3 Launcher that only loads:

Your master_patch module

The minimal set of required mods (Elf Destiny, Architect of Wonders, Carnalis if needed)

The CK3 base game
This isolates interactions.

Add files and quick-check
Paste one logical chunk (e.g., traits + modifiers) into the test mod.

Start the game with the test profile. Look for errors on load or missing localization warnings.

If the launcher complains about missing files/keys, check the console or game.log for the exact missing key.

Event testing
Add the events file. Run the game and trigger the event manually (use the console event numenor_mod.600100 <character id>) to see the full chain.

If an event doesnâ€™t fire, check the trigger conditions and localization keys.

Do the same for decisions (use decision NUMENOR_INITIATE_MIDNIGHT if needed with the console).

Wider compatibility
If basic tests pass, enable another small set of mods (2â€“5) that you think are most likely to interact (e.g., Elf Destiny, Carnalis). Repeat tests.

Gradually add more mods in batches, testing after each batch. This exposes conflicts incrementally.

Debug tools & logs
Check Documents/Paradox Interactive/Crusader Kings III/logs/game.log â€” errors, missing localization, and stack traces appear here.

In-game console commands: event <id> <char id>, decision <id>. These help trigger things without waiting.

Use a local copy of your events if you need to tweak and re-test quickly.

5) Common conflicts & how to fix them
Missing localization / blank titles
Symptom: events fire but show empty title or â€œROOTâ€ or localization key raw text.

Fix: ensure the localization key exactly matches and is in the correct file encoding (UTF-8 without BOM). Also ensure your .yml starts with l_english: header.

Event ID collision
Symptom: events trigger wrong text or wrong event triggers.

Fix: change your event ID block to a unique range (e.g., numenor_mod.600xxx).

Trait / decision overwritten by other mod
Symptom: your trait not applied or decision invisible.

Fix: unique id and check load order. If another mod redefines the same file path, move your file later in load order or give your trait a unique name. For hardened conflicts, create a compatibility patch that checks if mod X present then use alt key Y.

Overriding vanilla files unintentionally
Symptom: big behavior changes, UI errors.

Fix: undo overwriting of vanilla files; use append-only approach. If you must replace vanilla file, document and limit replacements.

6) Practical merge checklist (use before you push anything live)
 All keys prefixed numenor_ or anarion_?

 Event IDs in a safe, unused range (600000+)?

 Localization files utf-8 and l_english: header present?

 Decisions use unique IDs (caps, e.g., NUMENOR_INITIATE_MIDNIGHT)?

 No vanilla files edited unless absolutely necessary?

 README notes dependencies and load-order suggestions?

 Test profile created and passes basic event & decision triggers?

 game.log inspected for warnings/errors after test run?

 Backups saved of previous working mod state?

7) If things break â€” quick recovery steps
Disable the last file you added and re-run the game. If the error disappears, the problem is in that file.

Read game.log immediately after starting the game; look for errors in your file names or missing localization keys.

Fix the file, re-copy, and test again.

8) Tools & tips that make life easier
Use a simple diff tool (WinMerge, Meld) to compare current master_patch vs new changes.

Keep a single modlist.txt (manual) that records load order and notes.

Use a staging folder where you build modules, test them, then move to master_patch.

Keep your code modular â€” one feature = one file; one file = easy rollback.

start "" "%CK3_DIR%\binaries\ck3.exe"
exit

common/men_at_arms/twilight_men_at_arms.txt
# Twilight Legion men at arms
men_at_arms = {
    men_at_arms_twilight_legion = {
        picture = "gfx/interface/icons/men_at_arms/unit_twilight_legion.dds"
        type = light_infantry
        damage = 12
        tactics_bonuses = {
            defense = 0.10
            shock = 0.05
        }
        cost = 0.12
        upkeep = 0.10
        # flavor - magical component
        special = "twilight_vanguard_cohort"
    }

    men_at_arms_everguard = {
        picture = "gfx/interface/icons/men_at_arms/unit_everguard.dds"
        type = heavy_infantry
        damage = 20
        tactics_bonuses = {
            defense = 0.20
            assault = 0.10
        }
        cost = 0.20
        upkeep = 0.18
        # personal dynastic guard - cannot be raised by others via decisions
        special = "everguard_cohort"
    }
}
NOTE: numeric values are placeholders â€” tweak balance to fit your modlist.

common/court_positions/twilight_court_positions.txt

        prestige = 0.02
    }
    # icon placeholder
    icon = "gfx/interface/icons/positions/magister_supreme.dds"

        piety = 0.05
        monthly_scheme_power_add = 0.05
    }
    icon = "gfx/interface/icons/positions/grand_matriarch.dds"
}

    id = court_pos_imperial_archmage
    name = "Imperial Archmage"
    effect = {
        learning = 0.05
        martial = 0.02
    }
    icon = "gfx/interface/icons/positions/imperial_archmage.dds"
}

        personal_army_bonus = 0.05
    }
    icon = "gfx/interface/icons/positions/everguard_captain.dds"
}

events/twilight_legion_events.txt
This file contains multiple events: recruitment to Twilight Legion, awarding medals, Midnight Covenant recruit/assignment, and the newsletter triggers. Paste it as a single event file or split events if you like.

Important: The event language here is simplified CK3 event syntax. You may need to rename character_event to match your CK3 version or mod conventions.

# Twilight Legion + Midnight Covenant events

namespace = twilight_legion

# 1000: join Twilight Legion decision/event
character_event = {
    id = twilight_legion.1000
    desc = "twilight_legion.1000.desc"
    picture = GFX_evt_council_meeting
    trigger = {
        # example: adult, ruler or noble, martial > 10
        is_adult = yes
        NOT = { has_trait = trait_twilight_legionary_member }
        martial = 8
    }
    immediate = {
        # offer decision to join
    }
    option = {
        name = "Join the Legion"
        add_trait = trait_twilight_legionary_member
        prestige = 50
        custom_tooltip = "You are now eligible for Twilight Legion ranks."
    }
}

# 1010: award medal event (sample)
character_event = {
    id = twilight_legion.1010
    desc = "twilight_legion.1010.desc"
    picture = GFX_evt_honors
    trigger = {
        # placeholder: when granted by decision
    }
    immediate = {
        # add award logic (replace with correct game effect)
        add_award = award_medal_honor
        add_prestige = 50
    }
    option = {
        name = "Accept"
    }
}

# 2000: Midnight Covenant recruitment (assign codename)
character_event = {
    id = twilight_legion.2000
    desc = "twilight_legion.2000.desc"
    picture = GFX_evt_spy
    trigger = {
        is_adult = yes
        sex = female
        NOT = { has_trait = trait_midnight_covenant }
        # conditions to be shortlisted: beauty or intrigue or high intrigue lifestyle
    }
    immediate = {
        # assign trait and pick codename from pool stored as game variable -> simpler: pick random from list
        add_trait = trait_midnight_covenant
        # store codename in character custom name (using set_character_flag or dynamic name, simplified)
        # CK3 doesn't have direct "codename" field; use custom_trait with localisation or use character_name modifier.
    }
    option = {
        name = "Initiate"
    }
}

# 3000: Imperial Quill - example news trigger on coronation (fires a short newspaper event)
character_event = {
    id = twilight_legion.3000
    desc = "twilight_legion.3000.desc"
    trigger = {
        # example trigger: character becomes emperor (you)
    }
    immediate = {
        # add flavour: a decision is created which posts an article to all vassals or to player's event log
    }
    option = {
        name = "Publish"
    }
}
This is a template. CK3 event syntax is version-sensitive. Use this to plug into your event system and I can help refine line-by-line if any errors appear during game tests.

events/imperial_quill_events.txt

# Imperial Quill pseudo-events

    picture = GFX_evt_crowning
    trigger = { } # fired by scripted_action whenever coronation occurs
    immediate = { }

        name = "Read the Quill"
    }

# Example: an event the player can trigger (Decision) to broadcast the Quill
Implementation approach: Use on_actions to detect triggers (coronation, declare_war etc.) and call these events. Alternatively use decisions that the player chooses to publish an article and take small buffs.

common/on_actions/twilight_on_actions.txt
Hook sample: when ruler gets crowned -> trigger quill event.

on_action = {
    on_character_become_emperor_or_king = {
        effect = {
            character_event = { id = imperial_quill.100 scope = ROOT }
        }
    }
    # you can add more hooks: on_war_declared, on_province_construction, on_birth_heir, on_peace, etc.
}

1) Is a dynasty-only Everguard safe?
Short answer: itâ€™s risky but manageable.

Pros:

Absolute loyalty to dynasty (family protects family).

Very roleplay-cool: private royal guard, ceremonial and personal.

Cons:

Dynasty relatives can plot to seize power â€” if they control personal troops, they can stage coups.

Family members often have claims and factions. When succession struggles happen, dynasty-only guard can be a tool for rivals inside the family.

My recommendation (safe + roleplay):

Make most frontline/field units of the Everguard not permanently assigned as a private army â€” instead make them palace guard / household men-at-arms (defend court, personal bodyguard). Reduce their capacity to raise as an independent field army.

Allow some dynasts in the Everguard but mix in loyal non-dynasty officers (e.g., elite houses sworn to the Everking). Or make membership conditional: noble must swear a binding oath that removes claim or enforces penalties if they break it (mechanical enforcement via events).

Use rotation: members serve a term (e.g., 10 years) and then retire. This reduces long-term power consolidation.

Make the Captain of the Everguard appointed by you and removable by you (so no permanent autonomous commander).

Consider a secret loyalty check (event-driven) so you can purge or demote if someone looks dangerous.

PART 1 â€” Twilight Legion recruitment decision/event (paste this now)
Create a file at:
<your mod>/events/twilight_legion_recruitment.txt

Paste the entire block below exactly as-is (you can overwrite existing file of same name). This version is deliberately straightforward and uses generic triggers: it only offers the decision when the player is an Emperor (realm tier check), and itâ€™s attached to the player character via a decision-style event. If your CK3 version requires character_event vs on_action we can adapt later â€” this uses a decision-style event approach many mods support.

# twilight_legion_recruitment.txt
# Twilight Legion - Recruitment / Redemption Decision
# Paste into: <your mod>/events/twilight_legion_recruitment.txt

namespace = twilight_legion

# Decision-like event for recruiting to Twilight Legion
character_event = {
    id = twilight_legion.0100
    hide_window = no
    is_triggered_only = no

    trigger = {
        # Only appear for an Emperor-level ruler (empire formed)
        # Generic check for empire-tier realm; adjust if your CK3 version differs.
        realm_tier = empire
        is_ai = no
        is_player = yes
    }

    immediate = {
        # nothing immediate; display options
    }

    # Flavor text in localisation keys (see localisation file)
    desc = "twilight_legion.0100.desc"
    picture = GFX_evt_council_meeting

    option = {
        name = "twilight_legion.0100.opt.join_glorious" # Join gloriously
        # Glorious join: recipient gains the Legion trait and prestige
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
        add_trait = trait_twilight_legionary_member
        add_prestige = 100
        add_stability = 0
        custom_tooltip = "twilight_legion.0100.opt.join_glorious.tooltip"
    }

    option = {
        name = "twilight_legion.0100.opt.renounce_claim" # Renounce claim & join
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
        # Player chooses to renounce claim to throne and join the legion for honor
        # This uses a safe approach: remove claimant status and add trait
        remove_claim = yes
        add_trait = trait_twilight_legionary_member
        add_prestige = 150
        add_opinion = {
            who = ROOT
            modifier = 10
        }
        # We add a temporary 'renounced_heir' marker (used by other events)
        set_character_flag = has_renounced_claim_for_legion
        custom_tooltip = "twilight_legion.0100.opt.renounce_claim.tooltip"
    }

    option = {
        name = "twilight_legion.0100.opt.join_for_shame" # Shame redemption
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
        # Player accepts a period of service to restore honor instead of full privileges:
        add_trait = trait_twilight_legionary_member
        add_prestige = 50
        # Add a timed effect: a 'service' flag for 10 years (3650 days)
        set_character_flag = twilight_legion_service_active
        # you can later remove flag with an event that grants a medal
        custom_tooltip = "twilight_legion.0100.opt.join_for_shame.tooltip"
    }
}

# Character modifier(s) to lock down Everguard members (Phase 1)

    name = everguard_mod_fanatic_loyalty

        factor = 0
    }

ChatGPT said:
Great â€” Phase 1-A is pasted and done, so we continue with Phase 1-B exactly as promised.
(Iâ€™ll also answer your question about â€œtwo files inside the same mod editing the same thingâ€ right before giving you the next files.)

âœ… Before Phase 1-B â€” Your Questions Answered
Q: â€œWhat if two files INSIDE the same mod edit the same thing?â€
Inside a single mod, load-order problems disappear â€” BUT overwrites still happen.

Example
Suppose your mod has:

common/traits/zzz_trait_file_A.txt

common/traits/zzz_trait_file_B.txt

And both define the same trait, like:

trait = risky_trait {
   ...stuff...
}
Then whichever file is later alphabetically (B in this case) completely overwrites the first.
CK3 does not â€œmergeâ€ traits, culture items, buildings, men-at-arms entries, etc.

The rule is simple:

â­ Inside the same mod, last alphabetical file wins.
This is why I use prefixes like:

zzz_vss_...
Because:

They always load last.

They always overwrite the vanilla file.

They never overwrite each other unless we put duplicates by mistake.

And I avoid duplicates by designing everything clean.

Conclusion:
As long as every item (trait, culture parameter, interaction, reward, etc.) appears in exactly one zzz_vss_ file, we are 100% safe.

# 600001 - Midnight Initiation (ruler invites a courtier/maid)
# ---------------------------------------------------------
character_event = {
    id = numenor_mod.600001
    hide_window = no

    trigger = {
        is_ruler = yes
        dynasty = d_anarion
        any_title = { has_title = e_numenor } # module usually dormant until empire, but event can be used if you want
        NOT = { has_global_flag = numenor_midnight_initialized } # first-time global initialize check optional
    }

    title = "numenor_mod.600001.t"
    desc = "numenor_mod.600001.d"

    option = {
        name = "numenor_mod.600001.a_grant"
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
        # flavor: pick a courtier (maid) you own; here we add trait to ROOT.targeted_character by event caller
        add_prestige = 100
        set_global_flag = numenor_midnight_initialized
        news_event = { id = numenor_mod.600001.1 scope = ROOT }
        # The actual granting is done by decision which picks a character parameter (see decisions file)
    }

    option = {
        name = "numenor_mod.600001.b_decline"
        ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
        add_piety = 10
    }
}

The event-level logic (showing 5-name shortlist, handling the initiateâ€™s selection, etc.) will call these effects; Iâ€™ll send those events next after you confirm this file.

common/scripted_effects/numenor_codenames.txt

###############################################################
# common/scripted_effects/numenor_codenames.txt
# Numenor â€” Midnight Covenant codename & persona engine
# Effects used by initiation events and flavor systems.
#
# - numenor_set_codename: applies the codename as a visible nickname
#   and marks the character as a covenant member (non-destructive).
# - numenor_remove_codename: removes the codename nickname and flag.
# - numenor_assign_persona: assigns a persona flag (dignified, lustful, etc.)
#   based on existing traits; falls back to a random persona.
# - numenor_clear_persona: removes any persona flags.
#
# Notes:
# - This file intentionally avoids dynamic per-codename character_flags to
#   minimize compatibility issues with other mods. The codename itself is
#   stored as a nickname (custom text) and a simple boolean flag marks
#   "has been assigned".
# - Only player-triggered events should call these effects (AI will be blocked).
###############################################################

# Assign a codename to the scoped character (called from events)
numenor_set_codename = {
    parameter:codename = ""

    # Small safety guard: do nothing if codename empty
    if = {
        limit = { check_variable = { which = codename value = "" } }
        # no-op
    }
    else = {
        # remove any previous nickname of this special slot (clean)
        remove_nickname = { nickname = nick_covenant_codename }

        # Add the codename as a nickname: "Codename: $custom$"
        add_nickname = {
            nickname = nick_covenant_codename
            custom = codename
        }

        # Mark character as having a covenant codename assigned (simple flag)
        set_character_flag = numenor_codename_assigned

        # Slight hidden bonus: mark as part of the network (non-visible buff)
        add_character_modifier = { modifier = numenor_midnight_loyal days = -1 }
    }
}

# Remove codename (used when retiring/retiring-soft)
numenor_remove_codename = {
    # Remove the special nickname and clear the assigned flag
    remove_nickname = { nickname = nick_covenant_codename }
    clear_character_flag = numenor_codename_assigned

    # Remove persona flags and membership modifier if present
    remove_character_modifier = numenor_midnight_loyal
    numenor_clear_persona = { }
}

# Helper: clear all persona flags (scoped character)
numenor_clear_persona = {
    clear_character_flag = persona_dignified
    clear_character_flag = persona_tomboy
    clear_character_flag = persona_lustful
    clear_character_flag = persona_joyous
    clear_character_flag = persona_stoic
    clear_character_flag = persona_mischief
    clear_character_flag = persona_devoted
    clear_character_flag = persona_sadistic
    clear_character_flag = persona_huntress
}

# Assign a persona to the scoped character (tries trait heuristics first,
# otherwise falls back to a random persona). Personas influence flavor lines
# and the initiate's choice when presented with multiple codenames.
numenor_assign_persona = {
    # Clear any previous personas (safe re-assign)
    numenor_clear_persona = { }

    # Heuristic mapping by existing common traits (these are typical CK3 traits)
    # If multiple conditions are true, the first match wins (ordered by priority).
    if = {
        limit = { has_trait = trait_lustful }
        set_character_flag = persona_lustful
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_trait = trait_diligent }
        set_character_flag = persona_dignified
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_trait = trait_brave }
        set_character_flag = persona_tomboy
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_trait = trait_kind } # kind -> joyous/ domestic
        set_character_flag = persona_joyous
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_trait = trait_deceitful }
        set_character_flag = persona_mischief
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_trait = trait_proud }
        set_character_flag = persona_stoic
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_trait = trait_cruel }
        set_character_flag = persona_sadistic
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = { has_trait = trait_prowess } # fallback for martial types
        set_character_flag = persona_huntress
    }
    else = {
        # If no strong trait signals, pick randomly among the core personas.
        random = {
            chance = 15
            set_character_flag = persona_dignified
        }
        random = {
            chance = 15
            set_character_flag = persona_tomboy
        }
        random = {
            chance = 15
            set_character_flag = persona_lustful
        }
        random = {
            chance = 15
            set_character_flag = persona_joyous
        }
        random = {
            chance = 15
            set_character_flag = persona_mischief
        }
        random = {
            chance = 15
            set_character_flag = persona_stoic
        }
        random = {
            chance = 10
            set_character_flag = persona_sadistic
        }
    }
}

# Utility: return a persona tag name for localization or branching.
# (Event authors can test for persona flags directly; this effect just documents.)
numenor_persona_hint = {
    if = { limit = { has_character_flag = persona_dignified }  }
    else_if = { limit = { has_character_flag = persona_tomboy } }
    else_if = { limit = { has_character_flag = persona_lustful } }
    else_if = { limit = { has_character_flag = persona_joyous } }
    else_if = { limit = { has_character_flag = persona_mischief } }
    else_if = { limit = { has_character_flag = persona_stoic } }
    else_if = { limit = { has_character_flag = persona_sadistic } }
    else_if = { limit = { has_character_flag = persona_huntress } }
    else = { } # no-op
}

###############################################################
# End of numenor_codenames.txt
###############################################################

        }
